#=============================================================================
#=== PLC Fi3_FailOverInfo
#=====================================
OBJ: Fi3_FailOverInfo
  DIAG: v=3 s=MBT_DIAG
  CYCL: v=1
  PARL: P0=Fi3_MB_Enable
  FUNC: IF P0 : Q1; ELSE Q0;
#------------------------------
M:        p=42 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1751 S=Fi3_MB1_PLCLive    d=2

#=============================================================================
#=== PLC clock
#=====================================
OBJ: Fi3_ClockRead
  DIAG: v=3 s=MBT_DIAG
  CYCL: v=1
  PARL: P0=Fi3_MB1_Enable
  FUNC: IF P0 : Q1; ELSE Q0;
#------------------------------
M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1742 S=Fi3_PLCClkDayOfWeek
M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1743 S=Fi3_PLCClkMonth
M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1744 S=Fi3_PLCClkDay
M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1745 S=Fi3_PLCClkYear
M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1746 S=Fi3_PLCClkHour
M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1747 S=Fi3_PLCClkMin
M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1748 S=Fi3_PLCClkSec
M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1749 S=Fi3_PLCClkSet
M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1750 S=Fi3_PLCClkDec

M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1751 S=?

M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1752 S=Fi3_ConstSwpSt
M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1753 S=Fi3_ConstSwpAc
M:        p=41 t=HR o=I  f=W r=1754 S=Fi3_MaxSweepTm



#=============================================================================
#=== Setting PLC clock
#=====================================

#@Address: 5301
OBJ: Fi3_WritePLCClockContr
  DIAG: v=3 s=MBT_DIAG
  CYCL: v=0
  PARL: P0=Fi3_MB1_Enable P1=Fi3_WrtClkControl
  FUNC: IF P0 && S1: Q1; ELSE Q0;
#------------------------------
M:        p=45 t=HR o=O f=W r=4901 S=Fi3_WrtClkControl

OBJ: Fi3_WritePLCClock
  DIAG: v=3 s=MBT_DIAG
  CYCL: v=0
  PARL: P0=Fi3_MB1_Enable P1=Fi3_WrtClkDayOfWeek P2=Fi3_WrtClkMonth \
        P3=Fi3_WrtClkDay P4=Fi3_WrtClkYear P5=Fi3_WrtClkHour P6=Fi3_WrtClkMin \
        P7=Fi3_WrtClkSec
  FUNC: IF P0 && (S1|S2|S3|S4|S5|S6|S7) : Q1; ELSE Q0;
#------------------------------
M:        p=45 t=HR o=O f=W r=4902 S=Fi3_WrtClkDayOfWeek
M:        p=45 t=HR o=O f=W r=4903 S=Fi3_WrtClkMonth
M:        p=45 t=HR o=O f=W r=4904 S=Fi3_WrtClkDay
M:        p=45 t=HR o=O f=W r=4905 S=Fi3_WrtClkYear
M:        p=45 t=HR o=O f=W r=4906 S=Fi3_WrtClkHour
M:        p=45 t=HR o=O f=W r=4907 S=Fi3_WrtClkMin
M:        p=45 t=HR o=O f=W r=4908 S=Fi3_WrtClkSec
#@End


#=============================================================================
#=== The 'PC is working' signal
#=====================================
OBJ: Fi3_PCisWorking
  DIAG: v=3 s=MBT_DIAG
  CYCL: v=4
  PARL: P0=Fi3_MB1_Enable
  FUNC: IF P0 : Q1; ELSE Q0;
#------------------------------
#@Address: 5309
M:        p=45 t=HR o=O f=W r=4909 S=Dummy01_Fix1
#@End

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
#--- Fi3_Chain01
#---------------------------------------
OBJ: Fi3_Chain01InitWrite
  DIAG: v=3 s=MBT_DIAG
  CYCL: v=0
  PARL: P0=Q_Ch16ChainInit P1=Fi3_MB1_Enable
  FUNC: IF P0 && P1: Q1; ELSE Q0;
#------------------------------
#@Address: 5310
M:  p=41 t=HR o=O f=W r=4910 S=Dummy01_Fix1

OBJ: Fi3_Chain01InitRead
  DIAG: v=3 s=MBT_DIAG
  CYCL: v=1
  PARL: P0=Q_Ch16ChainInitTrg P1=Fi3_MB1_Enable
  FUNC: IF (P0&1) && P1 : Q1; ELSE Q0;
#  CYCL: v=0
#  PARL: P0=Q_Ch16ChainInitTrg P1=Fi3_MB1_Enable P2=SysClkSec
#  FUNC: IF (P0&1) && P1 && (S2==3): Q1; ELSE Q0;
#------------------------------
M:  p=41 t=HR o=I f=W r=4910 S=Q_Ch16ChainInit

OBJ: Fi3_Chain01AckWrite
  DIAG: v=3 s=MBT_DIAG
  CYCL: v=0
  PARL: P0=Q_Ch16ChainAck P1=Fi3_MB1_Enable
  FUNC: IF !P0 && P1: Q1;ELSE Q0;
#------------------------------
M:  p=41 t=HR o=O f=W r=4911 S=Q_Ch16ChainAck

OBJ: Fi3_Chain01AckRead
  DIAG: v=3 s=MBT_DIAG
  CYCL: v=0
  PARL: P0=Q_Ch16ChainInitTrg P1=Q_Ch16ChainAck P2=SysClkSec P3=Fi3_MB1_Enable
  FUNC: IF !P0 && !P1 && (S2==3) && P3: Q1;ELSE Q0;
#------------------------------
M:  p=41 t=HR o=I f=W r=4911 S=Q_Ch16ChainAck
#@End

OBJ: Fi3_Chain01QueueRead
  DIAG: v=3 s=MBT_DIAG
  CYCL: v=0
  PARL: P0=Q_Ch16ChainAckTrg P1=Fi3_MB1_Enable
  FUNC: IF P0 && P1: Q1; ELSE Q0;
#------------------------------
#@Address: 4492
M:  p=41 t=HR o=I f=W r=4373  S=Q_Ch16Queue000  n=119 d=2
#@End
